1.	FUND – Fundamental  (Fundamental level)
2.	MCP – Microsoft Certificate Professionals (Intermediate Level)
3.	MTA – Microsoft Technology Associate (Advanced Level)
I am herewith sharing 40 courses list along with the prerequisites information.
Please contact you respective HoD in order to enroll for the courses. Each student is eligible to register for a maximum of five courses. 
The duration of the course may vary from three to six months, depending on the course. However, there is no overlapping between regular class works and classes conducted by Microsoft. 
Please share this information in your respective class groups and share it to all your friends. 
PLEASE TREAT IT AS VERY IMPORTANT.
Tomorrow is the last date to Register. hurry up!!

8/25/22, 11:23 - Rihana CM: Dear Students,

Life is a gift that god has given to us. We should live it to the fullest. Do not take extreme decisions for small things. Sometimes, we may come across situations where we feel that there is no way in which we can overcome the problem. But, remember one thing i.e. for every problem, there will be a solution. We may not find it when we are depressed/ in deep sorrow. First of all, try to calm down then think of the solution. You will definitely find one. 
You may need just one hour to think of ending your life and do it. But your parents have to bare that pain till their last breath. Just think of people who are suffering with cancer and other deadly diseases. They are fighting for their lives even though they have minimal chance of living. Your problem is not at all bigger than your life. Hence, think twice before your take extreme decision. If you have any issues, kindly contact me. Do not hesitate. 
Note: If you observe any difference in your roommates' behavior, kindly bring it to the notice of Caretaker/Warden/ADSW/DSW immediately. PLEASE.

Greetings from IES !!

We are pleased to provide the linkage to German technology and bilateral relations to Indian colleges and universities for a decade and happy to have you as one of the unique values add parts in it.

We are happy to associate with you in building the German-India knowledge ecosystem and until now our focus is Robotics and Industry 4.0,and our initiatives have excelled the operation in fields of automation, robotics, and Industry 4.0 several students achieved better career opportunities in Germany/India.

We are also extremely happy and delighted to have APSSDC, the Government of Andhra Pradesh to support in this activity, and further this year we are having support from them to skill in different emerging technologies not only core but also in IT domain.

At this outset we have chosen one of the emerging topics "Data Science", we have designed 3 months internship program with live projects and hackathon.


Why Data Science?

Data is "Everything" in the current world, whatever course or job we are targeting, data analysis and data interpretation became essential in order to excel in respective jobs/careers.
This is going to be a foundational program for computer science engineers, even thereafter they want to become Artificial Intelligence Expert/BlockChain Expert/Machine learning experts and/or cyber security experts.
This is the reason we chose as the second topic of our second skill cluster and with this opportunity, we would like to invite you as part of this ADC (Advanced Data Science) Cluster.

Who is involved ?

Government initiatives, University, and industry experts are involved in delivering and funding the current program.

The current program is designed to Indian Industry experts along with experts from Kempten University Germany.


Uniqueness of the program & Benefits to student :

• 3 months program consisting - Live lectures from German University Professors from state universities , Live lectures from Industry experts and Industry oriented cases studies with International curriculum .
• Learn – Practice and Implement methodology & Opportunity to implement real-time case studies

• ASSDC and International certification
• German quality and quantitative learning practices
• Competition/Hackathon at the end of program
• Summer School, Internship, employment linked higher education opportunity in German universities
• Student will be encountering very minimum certification costs
• career and higher education opportunities to esteemed universities like Kempten University, Reutlingen University, and Steinbeis University - which has fellowship programs with companies like Mercedes, Porsche, SAP, SIEMENS, Salesforce, etc
•Uniqueness of the program & Benefits to COLLEGE:

Makes everything easier for college.

• Be a part of unique “ADC – Advanced Data Science Cluster”, get funded international-industry skilled program.

Improve capabilities

-FDP activities, networking with German professors and universities

• Networking to develop IGSTC-DST programs, ERASMUS, ERASMUS+ programs.

•We have a lot of experience in various projects.

• Participation of funded activity by APSSDC, Govt of AP and its German/International partners.

• Exploring the employment and research linkages to Germany

We wish to invite and consider your students as our partner university for this program and further in order to achieve any value additions like hackathons and any further international certification programs.
